| 1:21:44| a ratio of teachers to students for those various levels.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090126?start=4904)|
| 1:21:49| So we believe that that allows us to be very clear about what our allocation of resources is.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090126?start=4909)|

| 1:22:15| and transparent distribution of resources to schools.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090126?start=4935)|

| 1:28:00| Whereas Robert Jackson Hughley, the youngest of four children,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090126?start=5280)|
| 1:28:04| was born in Columbia, Tennessee in 1955 to a band director, big band leader, and music shop owner,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090126?start=5284)|
| 1:28:12| and whereas the Hughley family moved to Knoxville in 1961,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090126?start=5292)|
| 1:28:16| at which time Robert began his first grade at West Hills,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090126?start=5296)|
| 1:28:20| and whereas after Robert attended Bearden Middle School, Bearden High School,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090126?start=5300)|
| 1:28:24| and the University of Tennessee, and whereas Mr. Hughley has two children,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090126?start=5304)|
| 1:28:30| 24-year-old Hannah, who works at the Knox County Schools at Lonsdale Elementary,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090126?start=5310)|
| 1:28:35| and 23-year-old Evan, who is in South College Radiography Program,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090126?start=5315)|
| 1:28:41| and whereas Robert was born to music enthusiasts,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090126?start=5321)|
| 1:28:45| worked for Hughley's music shop, and opened the downtown West Branch in 1980,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090126?start=5325)|
| 1:28:51| and whereas in 1991, after 45 years of operating the largest music store in Tennessee,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090126?start=5331)|
| 1:28:57| Robert closed Hughley's music shop, and whereas, in addition to his love for music,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090126?start=5337)|
| 1:29:03| Robert also has a passion for basketball, and in 1993,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090126?start=5343)|

| 2:46:28| Under 40-1-11, the legislative body of this county, which is you all, make appointment of the judicial commissioner.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090126?start=9988)|
| 2:46:39| It's a legislative appointment.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090126?start=9999)|
